<strong>\n        Important Notes\n        <br/>\n       </strong>\n       Options &amp; CSS classes may change a bit with new version release.\nKeep checking the\n       <a href="#release-notes">\n        Release Notes\n       </a>\n       !\n       <br/>\n       <br/>\n       <strong>\n        Philosophy:\n       </strong>\n       Vue Cal tries to separate logic &amp; styles.\n       <br/>\n       For performance, simplified logic, readability, structure &amp; maintenance of your own code,\nwhat can be done via CSS should be done via CSS. CSS classes will help you style your events, cells, splits, etc.\n      </p>\n      <h2 class="headline mt-5">\n       <a href="#installation">\n        Installation\n       </a>\n       <a id="installation" name="installation">\n       </a>\n      </h2>\n      <p class="highlight warning">\n       <i aria-hidden="true" class="v-icon material-icons theme--light">\n        priority_high\n       </i>\n       Vue.js 2.5.18 or later is required.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       You have 2 options:\n       <em>\n        NPM\n       </em>\n       <strong class="mx-2">\n        or\n       </strong>\n       <span class="code">\n        &lt;script&gt;\n       </span>\n       tag.\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       Via NPM\n      </h3>\n      <pre class="ssh-pre mt-2" data-label="Shell" data-type="shell"><span class="keyword">npm</span> i --S vue-cal</pre>\n      <p>\n       Then import the component and use it:\n      </p>\n      <pre class="ssh-pre mt-2" data-label="Javascript" data-type="js"><span class="comment">// In your VueJS component.</span>\n<span class="keyword">import</span> <span class="variable">VueCal</span> <span class="keyword">from</span> <span class="quote">\'vue-cal\'</span>\n<span class="keyword">import</span> <span class="quote">\'vue-cal/dist/vuecal.css\'</span>\n<span class="punctuation">...</span>\n\n<span class="keyword">export</span> <span class="keyword">default</span> <span class="punctuation">{</span>\n  <span class="variable">components</span><span class="punctuation">:</span> <span class="punctuation">{</span> <span class="variable">VueCal</span> <span class="punctuation">},</span>\n  <span class="variable">data</span><span class="punctuation">:</span> <span class="punctuation">()</span> <span class="punctuation">=&gt;</span> <span class="punctuation">({</span>\n    <span class="punctuation">...</span>\n  <span class="punctuation">}),</span>\n  <span class="punctuation">...</span>\n<span class="punctuation">}</span>\n</pre>\n      <h3>\n       Via\n       <span class="code">\n        &lt;script&gt;\n       </span>\n       tag\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       Include the Vue Cal script in your document\n       <span class="code">\n        &lt;head&gt;\n       </span>\n       as follows:\n      </p>\n      <pre class="ssh-pre mt-4" data-label="HTML" data-type="html"><span class="punctuation">&lt;</span><span class="tag-name">head</span><span class="punctuation">&gt;</span>\n  ...\n  <span class="punctuation">&lt;</span><span class="tag-name">script</span> <span class="attribute">src</span><span class="punctuation">=</span><span class="quote">"https://unpkg.com/vue"</span><span class="punctuation">&gt;</span><span class="punctuation">&lt;/</span><span class="tag-name">script</span><span class="punctuation">&gt;</span>\n  <span class="punctuation">&lt;</span><span class="tag-name">script</span> <span class="attribute">src</span><span class="punctuation">=</span><span class="quote">"https://unpkg.com/vue-cal"</span><span class="punctuation">&gt;</span><span class="punctuation">&lt;/</span><span class="tag-name">script</span><span class="punctuation">&gt;</span>\n  <span class="punctuation">&lt;</span><span class="tag-name">link</span> <span class="attribute">href</span><span class="punctuation">=</span><span class="quote">"https://unpkg.com/vue-cal/dist/vuecal.css"</span> <span class="attribute">rel</span><span class="punctuation">=</span><span class="quote">"stylesheet"</span><span class="punctuation">&gt;</span>\n<span class="punctuation">&lt;/</span><span class="tag-name">head</span><span class="punctuation">&gt;</span></pre>\n      <p>\n       Then define the component to use in your template:\n      </p>\n      <pre class="ssh-pre mt-4" data-label="Javascript" data-type="js"><span class="comment">// In your VueJS component.</span>\n<span class="keyword">export</span> <span class="keyword">default</span> <span class="punctuation">{</span>\n  <span class="variable">components</span><span class="punctuation">:</span> <span class="punctuation">{</span> <span class="quote">\'vue-cal\'</span><span class="punctuation">:</span> <span class="variable">vuecal</span> <span class="punctuation">},</span>\n  <span class="punctuation">...</span>\n<span class="punctuation">}</span>\n</pre>\n      <h2 class="headline mt-5 pt-5">\n       <a href="#how-to-use">\n        How to use\n       </a>\n       <a id="how-to-use" name="how-to-use">\n       </a>\n      </h2>\n      <p class="highlight warning">\n       <i aria-hidden="true" class="v-icon material-icons theme--light">\n        priority_high\n       </i>\n       <p>\n        Wait! Before you dive in, make sure you place Vue Cal in a container that\n        <strong>\n         has a set height\n        </strong>\n        ! (not auto or initial)\n        <br/>\n        By default Vue Cal will take the full width &amp; height of its container if it has a set height.\n       </p>\n       <pre class="ssh-pre mt-2" data-type="html-vue"><span class="comment">&lt;!-- If the container has no height, set a height on vue-cal --&gt;</span>\n<span class="punctuation">&lt;</span><span class="tag-name">vue-cal</span> <span class="attribute">style</span><span class="punctuation">=</span><span class="quote">"height: 250px"</span><span class="punctuation">&gt;</span><span class="punctuation">&lt;/</span><span priority_high\n       </i>\n       For all the options details, refer to the\n       <a href="#api">\n        API\n       </a>\n       section.\n      </p>\n      <h4 class="title">\n       <a href="#ex--min-max-dates">\n        # Minimum / maximum dates &amp; single click to navigate\n       </a>\n       <a id="ex--min-max-dates" name="ex--min-max-dates">\n       </a>\n      </h4>\n      <p>\n       With the options\n       <span class="code">\n        minDate\n       </span>\n       &amp;\n       <span class="code">\n        maxDate\n       </span>\n       , you can set a\ntime range of selectable cells. All the cells before and after are still visible but\nwill be disabled and not selectable.\n       <br/>\n       You can still navigate through them with arrows.\n       <br/>\n       In this example, the minimum date is set to 15 days behind and the maximum date to\n15 days ahead.\n       <br/>\n      </p>\n      <p class="highlight tips">\n       <i aria-hidden="true" class="v-icon material-icons theme--light">\n        wb_incandescent\n       </i>\n       <strong class="ml-2">\n        Notes:\n       </strong>\n       <ul>\n        <li>\n         the min and max options accept a formatted string or plain Javascript Date object.\n        </li>\n        <li>\n         2 different CSS class are available on out of range cells:\n         <span class="code">\n          .before-min\n         </span>\n         &amp;\n         <span class="code">\n          .after-max\n         </span>\n         .\n        </li>\n       </ul>\n      </p>\n      <div class="my-2 ma-auto main-content v-card you choose to show the time in vue-cal, the current time of today\'s date will\nbe marked with a line (scroll to the current time to see it).\n       <br/>\n       The line position will be updated every time the calendar current view is re-rendered (by interacting).\n       <br/>\n       You can easily customize the now-line as you wish via CSS.\nChanging the line and arrow color is as easy as:\n       <br/>\n      </p>\n      <pre class="ssh-pre mt-4" data-label="CSS" data-type="css"><span class="selector">.vuecal__now-line </span><span class="punctuation">{</span><span class="attribute keyword">color</span><span class="punctuation">:</span> <span class="color" style="background-color: #06c;color: #fff">#06c</span><span class="punctuation">;}</span></pre>\n      <p>\n       If you don\'t want this feature you can simply hide it:\n       <span class="code">\n        .vuecal__now-line {display: none}\n       </span>\n       .\n       <br/>\n       This feature has no impact on performance.\n      </p>\n      <div class="my-2 ma-auto main-content v-card v-sheet theme--light" style="width: 360px; height: 360px; max-width: 100%;">\n       <div class="vuecal__flex vuecal  By default the selected date is today. But if you get lost in time travel, you can add\na Today button to select Today\'s date with the option\n       <span class="code">\n        today-button\n       </span>\n       .\n       <br/>\n       Like navigation arrows, there is also a slot to customize as you want.\n       <br/>\n       Bellow are the default Today button on the left and a custom one with icon and tooltip on the right.\n      </p>\n      <p class="ex--adding-a-today-button">\n       If you are not satisfied with the position of this button, you can also place it\noutside of Vue Cal like so:\n       <button class="today-button v-btn v-btn--outline v-btn--depressed v-btn--round v-btn--small theme--light primary--text" type="button">\n        <div class="v-btn__content">\n         Another Today Button\n        </div>\n       </button>\n       <br/>\n       You might want to change view as well when going to Today\'s date, here is an example how:\n       <a class="mx-1" class="title">\n       <a href="#ex--open-dialog-on-event-click">\n        # Open a dialog box on event click / dblclick\n       </a>\n       <a id="ex--open-dialog-on-event-click" name="ex--open-dialog-on-event-click">\n       </a>\n      </h4>\n      <p class="mb-2">\n       By passing a function to the option\n       <span class="code">\n        on-event-click\n       </span>\n       or\n       <span class="code">\n        on-event-dblclick\n       </span>\n       ,\nyou can control what happens when you click or double click an event - on any view where the events are displayed.\n       <br/>\n       The callback function you provide will receive 2 arguments:\n      </p>\n      <ul>\n       <li>\n        <span class="code">\n         event\n        </span>\n        : the clicked calendar event\'s object\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <span class="code">\n         e\n        </span>\n        : the associated javascript DOM event\n       </li>\n      </ul>\n      <p class="mt-3 highlight tips">\n       <i aria-hidden="true" class="v-icon material-icons theme--light">\n        wb_incandescent\n       </i>\n       You can set any custom attribute you want on an event, you will then be able to access it in the dialog box!\n       <br/>\n      </p>\n      <div class="my-2 ma-auto main-content v-card v-sheet theme--light" style="height: -\n        <span class="code">\n         years\n        </span>\n        ,\n        <span class="code">\n         year\n        </span>\n        &amp;\n        <span class="code">\n         month\n        </span>\n        views\n       </a>\n       <a id="ex--events-indicators" name="ex--events-indicators">\n       </a>\n      </h4>\n      <p class="mb-0">\n       When you define events the\n       <span class="code">\n        month\n       </span>\n       view will display an events count per day.\n       <br/>\n       You can use the option\n       <span class="code">\n </span>\n       views as well.\n       <br/>\n       You can customize the events count as you wish via CSS.\n      </p>\n      <p class="mt-3 layout align-center">\n       <span class="mr-2">\n      With the option\n       <span class="code">\n        events-on-month-view\n       </span>\n       , you can choose whether to display the events on the month view or not.\n       <br/>\n       <span class="code">\n        events-on-month-view\n       </span>\n       accepts a Boolean to show or hide, or the string \'\n       <span class="code">\n        short\n       </span>\n       \' to show only the event\'s title.\n       <br/>\n       If\n       <span class="code">\n        events-on-month-view\n       </span>\n       is set to\n       <span class="code">\n        true\n       </span>\n       , all the informations are displayed, you can then hide\nany event information via CSS.\n       <br/>\n       If you want all the cells to have the same height on this view, this is    </div>\n         <pre class="ssh-pre my-2 caption" data-type="html-vue"><span class="punctuation">&lt;</span><span class="tag-name">vue-cal</span> <span class="attribute">selected-date</span><span     </div>\n       </li>\n      </ol>\n      <p class="mt-3">\n       By default, event will be created with these attributes:\n      </p>\n      <pre class="ssh-pre mt-0" data-label="Javascript" data-type="js"><span class="punctuation">{</span>\n    <span class="variable">start</span><span class="punctuation">:</span> <span class="punctuation">{</span><span class="keyword">String</span><span class="punctuation">},</span> <span class="comment">// (Formatted date) starting from your cursor position in the day cell you clicked.</span>\n    <span class="variable">end</span><span class="punctuation">:</span> <span class="punctuation">{</span><span class="keyword">String</span><span class="punctuation">},</span> <span class="comment">// (Formatted date) Event start + 2 hours</span>\n    <span class="variable">title</span><span class="punctuation">:</span> <span class="quote">\'\'</span><span class="punctuation">,</span>\n    <span you clicked.</span>\n<span class="punctuation">}</span>\n</pre>\n      <p>\n       If you want to customize those attributes you can modify the event directly through\nthe callback function that you provide to\n       <span class="code">\n        :on-event-create\n       </span>\n       as follows:\n       <br/>\n      </p>\n      <pre class="ssh-pre mt-4" data-label="Javascript" data-type="js"><span class="comment">// :on-event-create="onEventCreate", in template.</span>\n\n<span class="comment">/**\n * @param event {Object} The newly created event that you can override.\n * @param deleteEventFunction {Function} Allows you to delete this event programmatically.\n * @return {Object} The event to be passed back to Vue Cal.\n */</span>\n<span class="variable">onEventCreate</span> <span class="punctuation">(</span><span class="variable">event</span><span class="punctuation">,</span> <span class="variable">deleteEventFunction</span><span class="punctuation">)</span> <span class="punctuation">{</span>\n    <span class="comment">// You can modify event here and return it.</span>\n    <span class="keyword">return</span> <span class="variable">event</span>\n  <span class="punctuation">}</span>\n</pre>\n      <p>\n       Alternatively, like in this example, you can give the user the freedom to set a title,\ncontent, CSS class="punctuation">}</span>\n<span class="punctuation">}</span>\n</pre>\n      <h4 class="title">\n       <a href="#ex--multiple-day-events">\n        # Multiple day events\n       </a>\n       <a id="ex--multiple-day-events" name="ex--multiple-day-events">\n       </a>\n      </h4>\n      <p>\n       Multiple day events are working like a set of single day events linked together.\n       <br/>\n       Deleting one of the day of a multiple day event, will also delete all the other days.\n       <br/>\n       Updating the duration by dragging or changing the title will also update on all the days.\n       <br/>\n       Try to resize, rename and delete the events.\n      </p>\n      <p class="highlight tips">\n       <i aria-hidden="true" class="v-icon material-icons theme--light">\n        wb_incandescent\n       </i>\n       3 CSS classes are available to target the event first day, the last day and all the days in between:\n       <span class="code">\n        event-start\n       </span>\n       ,\n       <span class="code">\n        event-middle\n       </span>\n       ,\n       <span class="code">\n        event-end\n       </span>\n       .\n      </p>\n    <h4 class="title">\n       <a href="#ex--background-events">\n        # Background events\n       </a>\n       <a id="ex--background-events" name="ex--background-events">\n       </a>\n      </h4>\n      <p>\n       Just add the property\n       <span class="code">\n        background: true\n       </span>\n       to your events.\n       <br/>\n       The particularity of background events is that they can fully be overlapped but not overlapping.\n       <br/>\n       And they don\'t overlap like other events: when overlapping both events won\'t change width.\n       <br/>\n       Note that you can still select a background event to put it on top of others and see it.\nRefer to the\n       <span class="code">\n        events\n       </span>\n       option in the\n       <a href="#api">\n        API\n       </a>\n       section.\n      </p>\n      <div class="my-2 ma-auto main-content v-card v-sheet theme--light">\n       <div class="vuecal__flex vuecal  When the\n        <span class="code">\n         showAllDayEvents\n        </span>\n        is set to\n        <span class="code">\n         true\n        </span>\n        the events with an\n        <span class="code">\n         allDay\n        </span>\n        attribute set to\n        <span class="code">\n         true\n        </span>\n        will be displayed in a fixed top\nbar on the\n        <span class="code">\n         week\n        </span>\n        &amp;\n        <span class="code">\n         day\n        </span>\n        views.\n        <br/>\n        The all day events bar will only show up if the options\n        <span class="code">\n         showAllDayEvents\n        </span>\n        &amp;\n        <span class="code">\n         time\n        </span>\n        are set to\n        <span class="code">\n         true\n        </span>\n        .\n        <br/>\n        <span class="code">\n         time\n        </span>\n        is important since without time information every event is an all-day\nevent there is no point in separating them then.\n       </li>\n       <li class="mb-2">\n        When\n        <span class="code">\n         showAllDayEvents\n        </span>\n        is set to\n        <span class="code">\n         false\n        </span>\n        , all the all day events\n(\n        <span class="code">\n         allDay\n        </span>\n        attribute set to\n        <span class="code">\n         true\n        </span>\n        ), will show up as a normal\nbackground event.\n       </li>\n       <li class="mb-2">\n        On month view, switching\n        <span class="code">\n         showAllDayEvents\n        </span>\n        on and off will not have any impact\nsince both should display the all day events.\n       </li>\n       <li class="mb-2">\n        <span class="code">\n         showAllDayEvents\n        </span>\n        accepts a\n        <span class="code">\n         Boolean\n        </span>\n        or the string\n        <span class="code">\n         \'short\'\n        </span>\n        , to display only the event title.\n       </li>\n      </ul>\n      <p class="highlight info">\n       <i aria-hidden="true" class="v-icon material-icons theme--light">\n        priority_high\n       </i>\n       Multiple-day events feature will be improved in a future version to display across\nmultiple cells in the all day bar.\n      </p>\n      <button class="v-btn v-btn--small theme--light primary" type="button">\n       <div class="v-btn__content">\n        <span class="code">\n         :show-all-day-events="\'short\'"\n        </span>\n       </div>\n      </button>\n      <button class="v-btn v-btn--small theme--light primary" type="button">\n       <div class="v-btn__content">\n        <span class="code">\n         :events-on-month-views="true"\n        </span>\n       </div>\n      </button>\n      <div class="my-2 ma-auto main-content v-card v-sheet theme--light">\n    # Splitting days &amp; split events\n       </a>\n       <a id="ex--splitting-days" name="ex--splitting-days">\n       </a>\n      </h4>\n      <p class="mb-4">\n       Split each day into multiple containers passing a CSS class &amp; a label per split, and allow split-specific events.\n       <br/>\n       disabled views: years, year, month.\n       <br/>\n       On week view you can also overflow your content using a min-width on cells, like in this example, or fit to container:\n       <button class="v-btn v-btn--small theme--light primary" type="button">\n        <div class="v-btn__content">\n         <i aria-hidden="true" class="v-icon mr-2 material-icons theme--light">\n          remove\n         </i>\n         fit to container\n        </div>\n       </button>\n       <br/>\n       Refer to the\n       <span class="code">\n        splitDays\n       </span>\n       option in the\n       <a href="#api">\n        API\n       </a>\n       section.\n      </p>\n     <h4 class="title">\n       <a href="#ex--emitted-events">\n        # Vue Cal emitted events\n       </a>\n       <a id="ex--emitted-events" name="ex--emitted-events">\n       </a>\n      </h4>\n      <p class="mb-0">\n       Vue Cal emits events that you can listen to, to trigger an action outside of Vue Cal.\n       <br/>\n       If you are not familiar with Vue JS events, you should read about it here:\n       <a href="https://vuejs.org/v2/guide/events.html" target="_blank">\n        vuejs.org/v2/guide/events.html\n        <i aria-hidden="true" class="v-icon material-icons theme--light primary--text" style="font-size: 16px;">\n         open_in_new\n        </i>\n       </a>\n       <br/>\n       <br/>\n       Here is the list of emitted events:\n      </p>\n      <h4 class="mt-2">\n       View-related\n      </h4>\n      <ul>\n       <li>\n        <span class="code">\n         ready\n        </span>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <span class="code">\n         view-change\n        </span>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <span class="code">\n         cell-click\n        </span>\n        - is a JS native\n        <span class="code">\n         Date\n        </span>\n        object\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <span class="code">\n         cell-focus\n        </span>\n        - is a JS native\n        <span class="code">\n         Date\n        </span>\n        object\n       </li>\n      </ul>\n      <p class="highlight info">\n       <!-- -->\n       <span class="code">\n        cell-click\n       </span>\n       is fired every time you click a day, whereas\n       <span class="code">\n        cell-focus\n       </span>\n       is fired only when the selected day changes.\n      </p>\n      <p class="highlight info">\n       <!-- -->\n       The emitted events\n       <span class="code">\n        ready\n       </span>\n       &amp;\n       <span class="code">\n        view-change\n       </span>\n       return an object:\n       <br/>\n       <pre class="ssh-pre mt-2" data-type="js"><span class="punctuation">{</span>\n  <span class="variable">view</span><span class="punctuation">:</span> <span class="punctuation">[</span><span class="keyword">String</span><span class="punctuation">],</span>\n  <span class="variable">startDate</span><span class="punctuation">:</span> <span class="punctuation">[</span><span class="keyword">Date</span><span class="punctuation">],</span> <span class="comment">// View start - JS native Date object.</span>\n  <span class="variable">endDate</span><span class="punctuation">:</span> <span class="punctuation">[</span><span class="keyword">Date</span><span class="punctuation">],</span> <span class="comment">// View end - JS native Date object.</span>\n  <span class="variable">firstCellDate</span><span class="punctuation">:</span> <span class="punctuation">[</span><span class="keyword">Date</span><span class="punctuation">],</span> <span class="comment">// Month view only, in case cell is out of current month - JS native Date object.</span>\n  <span class="variable">lastCellDate</span><span class="punctuation">:</span> <span class="punctuation">[</span><span class="keyword">Date</span><span class="punctuation">],</span> <span class="comment">// Month view only, in case cell is out of current month - JS native Date object.</span>\n  <span class="variable">outOfScopeEvents</span><span class="punctuation">:</span> <span class="punctuation">[</span><span class="keyword">Array</span><span class="punctuation">],</span> <span class="comment">// Month view only, all the events that are out of the current month.</span>\n  <span class="variable">events</span><span class="punctuation">:</span> <span class="punctuation">[</span><span class="keyword">Array</span><span class="punctuation">],</span> <span class="comment">// All the events in the current view.</span>\n  <span class="variable">week</span><span class="punctuation">:</span> <span class="punctuation">[</span><span class="keyword">Integer</span><span class="punctuation">]</span> <span class="comment">// Week number. Only returned if view is \'week\'.</span>\n<span class="punctuation">}</span></pre>\n       <strong>\n        Note that on a month view, the events from the out of scope days\n(cells before and after the current month) are also returned in the array.\n       </strong>\n      </p>\n      <h4 class="mt-2">\n       Events-related\n      </h4>\n      <p class="mb-0">\n       In all events, properties\n       <span class="code">\n        startDate\n       </span>\n       &amp;\n       <span class="code">\n        endDate\n       </span>\n       are JS native\n       <span class="code">\n        Date\n       </span>\n       objects:\n      </p>\n      <ul>\n       <li>\n        <span class="code">\n         event-focus\n        </span>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <span class="code">\n         event-mouse-enter\n        </span>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <span class="code">\n         event-mouse-leave\n        </span>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <span class="code">\n         event-create\n        </span>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <span class="code">\n         event-delete\n        </span>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <span class="code">\n         event-change\n        </span>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <span class="code">\n         event-title-change\n        </span>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <span class="code">\n         event-content-change\n        </span>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <span class="code">\n         event-duration-change\n        </span>\n       </li>\n      </ul>\n      <p class="highlight tips">\n       <i aria-hidden="true" class="v-icon material-icons theme--light">\n        wb_incandescent\n       </i>\n       <ul>\n        <li>\n         The\n         <span class="code">\n          event-change\n         </span>\n         emitted event groups all the events triggered on a calendar event property change:\n         <span class="code">\n          event-title-change\n         </span>\n         ,\n         <span class="code">\n          event-content-change\n         </span>\n         ,\n         <span class="code">\n          event-duration-change\n         </span>\n         . So you have the choice to listen to\n         <span class="code">\n          event-change\n         </span>\n         to cover any calendar event change or listen to a specific action emitted event.\n        </li>\n        <li class="mt-3">\n         To help you manipulate an event\'s date, vue-cal returns native\n         <span class="code">\n          Date\n         </span>\n         objects in the event properties\n         <span class="code">\n          startDate\n         </span>\n         &amp;\n         <span class="code">\n          endDate\n         </span>\n         .\n         <br/>\n         So for instance, you can easily access the day of the week of an event with\n         <span class="code">\n          event.startDate.getDay()\n         </span>\n         .\n        </li>\n       </ul>\n      </p>\n      <p class="mb-0">\n       Watch the list of emitted events (latest on top) as you play with Vue Cal:\n      </p>\n      <pre class="mt-2 ssh-pre mb-2"><div <br/>\n       (Refer to the next example to know more:\n       <a href="#ex--custom-title-and-cells">\n        Custom title &amp; cells\n       </a>\n       )\n      </p>\n      <pre class="ssh-pre keyword">display</span><span class="punctuation">:</span> <span class="value keyword">block</span><span class="punctuation">;</span>\n<span class="punctuation">}</span>\n</pre>\n      <h4 class="title">\n       <a href="#ex--custom-title-and-cells">\n        # Custom title &amp; cells\n       </a>\n       <a id="ex--custom-title-and-cells" name="ex--custom-title-and-cells">\n       </a>\n      </h4>\n      <p class="highlight tips">\n       <i aria-hidden="true" class="v-icon material-icons theme--light">\n        wb_incandescent\n       </i>\n       <ul>\n        <li>\n         Using Vue.js scoped slots, you can override the calendar main date title and calendar cells.\n         <br/>\n         if you are not familiar with scoped slots and destructuring slot-scope, you should first read about it:\n         <a href="https://vuejs.org/v2/guide/components-slots.html#Scoped-Slots" target="_blank">\n          vuejs.org/v2/guide/components-slots.html\n          <i aria-hidden="true" class="v-icon material-icons theme--light primary--text" style="font-size: 16px;">\n           open_in_new\n          </i>\n         </a>\n        </li>\n        <li>\n         <strong>\n          Mind the difference of syntax for scoped slots since version 2.6.0 of Vue.js.\n         </strong>\n        </li>\n       </ul>\n      </p>\n      <h5 class="mt-4 subheading font-weight-medium">\n       <i aria-hidden="true" class="v-icon material-icons theme--light" style="font-size: 22px;">\n        keyboard_arrow_right\n       </i>\n       Custom title\n      </h5>\n      <p class="ml-2 mb-2">\n       2 arguments are available through the scoped slot:\n       <span class="code">\n        slot-scope="{ title, view }"\n       </span>\n      </p>\n      <ul>\n       <li>\n        <span class="code">\n         title\n        </span>\n        , the formatted title (different on all the views). E.g.\n        <em class="ml-2">\n         "Week 2 (January 2019)"\n        </em>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <span class="code">\n         view\n        </span>\n        , an object containing the active view info.\n        <pre class="ssh-pre mt-2 mb-3" data-type="js"><span class="punctuation">{</span>\n  <span class="variable">id</span><span class="punctuation">:</span> <span class="punctuation">{</span><span class="keyword">String</span><span class="punctuation">},</span> <span class="comment">// Current view, one of: years, year, month, week, day.</span>\n  <span class="variable">startDate</span><span class="punctuation">:</span> <span class="punctuation">{</span><span class="keyword">Date</span><span class="punctuation">},</span> <span class="comment">// JavaScript Date object.</span>\n  <span class="variable">endDate</span><span class="punctuation">:</span> <span class="punctuation">{</span><span class="keyword">Date</span><span class="punctuation">},</span> <span class="comment">// JavaScript Date object.</span>\n  <span class="variable">selectedDate</span><span class="punctuation">:</span> <span class="punctuation">{</span><span class="keyword">Date</span><span class="punctuation">}</span> <span class="comment">// JavaScript Date object.</span>\n<span class="punctuation">}</span></pre>\n       </li>\n      </ul>\n      <p>\n       You can use one or the other to format the title as you wish.\n       <br/>\n       Using the pre-formatted\n       <span class="code">\n        title\n       </span>\n       will be easy but not very flexible.\n       <br/>\n       If you render the date yourself from\n       <span class="code">\n        view.startDate\n       </span>\n       , don\'t forget\nthe different formats for all the views: years, year, month, week, day.\n      </p>\n      <h5 class="mt-4 subheading font-weight-medium">\n       <i aria-hidden="true" class="v-icon material-icons theme--light" style="font-size: 22px;">\n        keyboard_arrow_right\n       </i>\n       Custom cells\n      </h5>\n      <p class="ml-2 mb-2">\n       In this example, only the cell number is clickable on month view.\n       <br/>\n       5 arguments are available through the scoped slot:\n       <br/>\n       <span class="code">\n        slot-scope="{ cell, view, split, events, goNarrower }"\n       </span>\n      </p>\n      <ul>\n       <li>\n        <span class="code">\n         cell\n        </span>\n        , object containing the cell date.\n        <pre class="ssh-pre mt-2 mb-2" data-type="js"><span class="punctuation">{</span>\n  <span class="variable">content</span><span class="punctuation">:</span> <span class="punctuation">{</span><span class="keyword">String</span><span class="punctuation">},</span> <span class="comment">// Pre-formatted cell content if any.</span>\n  <span class="variable">startDate</span><span class="punctuation">:</span> <span class="punctuation">{</span><span class="keyword">Date</span><span class="punctuation">},</span> <span class="comment">// JavaScript Date object.</span>\n  <span class="variable">endDate</span><span class="punctuation">:</span> <span class="punctuation">{</span><span class="keyword">Date</span><span class="punctuation">},</span> <span class="comment">// JavaScript Date object.</span>\n  <span class="variable">formattedDate</span><span class="punctuation">:</span> <span class="punctuation">{</span><span class="keyword">String</span><span class="punctuation">},</span> <span class="comment">// formatted start date. E.g. "2019-04-05".</span>\n  <span class="variable">today</span><span class="punctuation">:</span> <span class="punctuation">{</span><span class="keyword">Boolean</span><span class="punctuation">}</span>\n<span class="punctuation">}</span></pre>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <span class="code">\n         view\n        </span>\n        , object containing the active view info.\n        <pre class="ssh-pre mt-2 mb-2" data-type="js"><span class="punctuation">{</span>\n  <span class="variable">id</span><span class="punctuation">:</span> <span class="punctuation">{</span><span class="keyword">String</span><span class="punctuation">},</span> <span class="comment">// Current view, one of: years, year, month, week, day.</span>\n  <span class="variable">startDate</span><span class="punctuation">:</span> <span class="punctuation">{</span><span class="keyword">Date</span><span class="punctuation">},</span> <span class="comment">// JavaScript Date object.</span>\n  <span class="variable">endDate</span><span class="punctuation">:</span> <span class="punctuation">{</span><span class="keyword">Date</span><span class="punctuation">},</span> <span class="comment">// JavaScript Date object.</span>\n  <span class="variable">selectedDate</span><span class="punctuation">:</span> <span class="punctuation">{</span><span class="keyword">Date</span><span class="punctuation">}</span> <span class="comment">// JavaScript Date object.</span>\n<span class="punctuation">}</span></pre>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <span class="code">\n         split\n        </span>\n        , when splitting days, object containing the current split info.\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <span class="code">\n         events\n        </span>\n        , array containing all the events of the current cell or split.\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <span class="code">\n         goNarrower\n        </span>\n        , function to navigate to narrower view if possible.\n       </li>\n      </ul>\n      <p class="my-3 highlight info">\n       <i aria-hidden="true" class="v-icon material-icons theme--light">\n        priority_high\n       </i>\n       By default a cell is rendered as follows.\n       <br/>\n       It is a good idea to reuse the same CSS classes as the different elements have associated styles:\n       <br/>\n       <pre class="ssh-pre mt-3 mb-1" data-type="html-vue"><span class="punctuation">&lt;</span><span class="tag-name">div</span> <span class="attribute">class</span><span class="punctuation">=</span><span class="quote">"vuecal__flex vuecal__cell-content"</span><span class="punctuation">&gt;</span></pre>\n       <pre class="ssh-pre my-2 ml-5" data-type="html-vue">Now this is the part you can customize:\n\n<span class="comment">&lt;!-- Will be added if splitting days and split labels are set --&gt;</span>\n<span class="punctuation">&lt;</span><span class="tag-name">div</span> <span class="attribute">class</span><span class="punctuation">=</span><span class="quote">"split-label"</span> <span class="punctuation">/&gt;</span>\n<span class="comment">&lt;!-- Will be added on years, year &amp; month view --&gt;</span>\n<span class="punctuation">&lt;</span><span class="tag-name">div</span> <span class="attribute">class</span><span class="punctuation">=</span><span class="quote">"vuecal__cell-date"</span> <span class="punctuation">/&gt;</span>\n<span class="comment">&lt;!-- Will be added on month view --&gt;</span>\n<span class="punctuation">&lt;</span><span class="tag-name">div</span> <span class="attribute">class</span><span class="punctuation">=</span><span class="quote">"vuecal__cell-events-count"</span> <span class="punctuation">/&gt;</span>\n<span class="comment">&lt;!-- Will be added on week and day view if no event --&gt;</span>\n<span class="attribute">slot-scope</span><span class="punctuation">=</span><span class="quote">"{ cell, view, events, goNarrower }"</span><span class="punctuation">&gt;</span>\n    <span class="punctuation">&lt;</span><span class="tag-name">span</span> <span class="attribute">class</span><span class="punctuation">=</span><span class="quote">"vuecal__cell-date"</span> <span class="attribute">:class</span><span class="punctuation">=</span><span class="quote">"view.id"</span> <span class="attribute">v-if</span><span class="punctuation">=</span><span class="quote">"view.id === \'day\'"</span> @<span class="attribute">click</span><span class="punctuation">=</span><span class="quote">"goNarrower"</span><span class="punctuation">&gt;</span>\n      {{ cell.date.getDate() }}\n    <span class="punctuation">&lt;/</span><span class="tag-name">span</span><span class="punctuation">&gt;</span>\n    <span class="punctuation">&lt;</span><span class="tag-name">span</span> <span class="attribute">class</span><span class="punctuation">=</span><span class="quote">"vuecal__cell-events-count"</span> <span class="attribute">v-if</span><span class="punctuation">=</span><span class="quote">"view.id === \'month\' &amp;&amp; events.length"</span><span class="punctuation">&gt;</span>{{ events.length }}<span class="punctuation">&lt;/</span><span class="tag-name">span</span><span class="punctuation">&gt;</span>\n    <span class="punctuation">&lt;</span><span class="tag-name">span</span> <span class="attribute">class</span><span class="punctuation">=</span><span class="quote">"vuecal__no-event"</span> <span class="attribute">v-if</span><span class="punctuation">=</span><span class="quote">"[\'week\', \'day\'].includes(view.id) &amp;&amp; !events.length"</span><span class="punctuation">&gt;</span>Nothing here \xf0\x9f\x91\x8c<span class="punctuation">&lt;/</span><span class="tag-name">span</span><span class="punctuation">&gt;</span>\n  <span class="punctuation">&lt;/</span><span class="tag-name">div</span><span class="punctuation">&gt;</span>\n\n  <span class="comment">&lt;!-- Alternatively to custom cells if you just want custom no-event text: --&gt;</span>\n  <span class="comment">&lt;!-- &lt;div slot="no-event"&gt;Nothing here \xf0\x9f\x91\x8c&lt;/div&gt; --&gt;</span>\n<span class="punctuation">&lt;/</span><span class="tag-name">vue-cal</span><span class="punctuation">&gt;</span>\n</pre>\n      <h4 class="title">\n       <a href="#ex--custom-event-rendering">\n        # Custom event rendering\n       </a>\n       <a id="ex--custom-event-rendering" name="ex--custom-event-rendering">\n       </a>\n      </h4>\n      <p class="mb-2">\n       Using Vue.js scoped slots, you can override the events rendering.\n      </p>\n      <p class="my-2 highlight tips">\n       <i aria-hidden="true" class="v-icon material-icons theme--light">\n        wb_incandescent\n       </i>\n       <ul>\n        <li>\n         If you are not familiar with scoped slots and destructuring slot-scope, you should first read about it:\n         <a href="https://vuejs.org/v2/guide/components-slots.html#Scoped-Slots" target="_blank">\n          vuejs.org/v2/guide/components-slots.html\n          <i aria-hidden="true" class="v-icon material-icons theme--light primary--text" style="font-size: 16px;">\n           open_in_new\n          </i>\n         </a>\n         .\n        </li>\n        <li>\n         <strong>\n          Mind the difference of syntax for scoped slots since version 2.6.0 of Vue.js.\n         </strong>\n        </li>\n       </ul>\n      </p>\n      <p class="my-3 highlight info">\n       <i aria-hidden="true" class="v-icon material-icons theme--light">\n        priority_high\n       </i>\n       By default an event is rendered as follows.\n       <br/>\n       It is a good idea to reuse the same CSS classes as the different elements have associated styles:\n       <br/>\n       <pre class="ssh-pre mt-3 mb-1" data-type="html-vue"><span class="punctuation">&lt;</span><span class="tag-name">div</span> <span class="attribute">class</span><span class="punctuation">=</span><span class="quote">"vuecal__event"</span><span class="punctuation">&gt;</span>\n    <span class="comment">&lt;!-- Will be added if `editable-events` option is set to `true` --&gt;</span>\n    <span class="punctuation">&lt;</span><span class="tag-name">div</span> <span class="attribute">class</span><span class="punctuation">=</span><span class="quote">"vuecal__event-delete"</span> <span class="punctuation">/&gt;</span></pre>\n       <pre class="ssh-pre my-2 ml-5" data-type="html-vue">Now this is the part you can customize:\n\n<span class="comment">&lt;!-- Will be added if a title is set --&gt;</span>\n<span class="punctuation">&lt;</span><span class="tag-name">div</span> <span class="attribute">class</span><span class="punctuation">=</span><span class="quote">"vuecal__event-title"</span> <span class="punctuation">/&gt;</span>\n<span class="comment">&lt;!-- or if title is set and `editable-events` option is set to `true` --&gt;</span>\n<span class="punctuation">&lt;</span><span class="tag-name">div</span> <span class="attribute">class</span><span class="punctuation">=</span><span class="quote">"vuecal__event-title vuecal__event-title--edit"</span> <span class="attribute">contenteditable</span> <span class="punctuation">/&gt;</span>\n\n<span class="comment">&lt;!-- Will be added if `time` option is set to `true` --&gt;</span>\n<span class="punctuation">&lt;</span><span class="tag-name">div</span> <span class="attribute">class</span><span class="punctuation">=</span><span class="quote">"vuecal__event-time"</span> <span class="punctuation">/&gt;</span>\n\n<span class="comment">&lt;!-- Will be added if a content is set --&gt;</span>\n<span class="punctuation">&lt;</span><span class="tag-name">div</span> <span class="attribute">class</span><span class="punctuation">=</span><span class="quote">"vuecal__event-content"</span> <span class="punctuation">/&gt;</span></pre>\n       <pre class="ssh-pre my-1" data-type="html-vue">    <span class="comment">&lt;!-- Will be added if `editable-events` option is set to `true` --&gt;</span>\n    <span class="punctuation">&lt;</span><span class="tag-name">div</span> <span class="attribute">class</span><span class="punctuation">=</span><span class="quote">"vuecal__event-resize-handle"</span> <span class="punctuation">/&gt;</span>\n<span class="punctuation">&lt;/</span><span class="tag-name">div</span><span class="punctuation">&gt;</span></pre>\n      </p>\n      <p class="mb-2">\n       Two parameters are passed through the scoped slot:\n      </p>\n      <ul>\n       <li>\n        <span class="code">\n         event\n        </span>\n        : The event full object containing dates, time, title, content and custom attributes.\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <span class="code">\n         view\n        </span>\n        : The current selected view id.\n       </li>\n      </ul>\n      <p class="mt-2">\n       You can set any custom attribute you want on an event, they will then be accessible in your custom event renderer!\n       <br/>\n       Note that\n       <span class="code">\n        _eid\n       </span>\n       is a reserved keyword.\n      </p>\n      <div class="my-2 ma-auto main-content v-card v-sheet theme--light" style="height: 523px;">\n       <div class="vuecal__flex vuecal vuecal--green-theme ex--custom-event-rendering locale\n        </code>\n        <span class="code">\n         [String], default: \'en\'\n        </span>\n        <p>\n         Allows you to translate the calendar texts in a given language.\n         <br/>\n         Use a 2 letter locale code (ISO 639-1) unless a distinction is needed. E.g.\n         <span class="code">\n          \'pt-br\'\n         </span>\n         for Portuguese-Brasilian.\n        </p>\n        <p class="highlight info">\n         <i aria-hidden="true" class="v-icon material-icons theme--light">\n          priority_high\n         </i>\n         Currently available languages are Arabic, Bosnian, Bulgarian, Catalan, Czech, Chinese (Simplified), Chinese (Traditional), Croatian, Danish, Dutch, English, Farsi, French, Georgian, German, Hebrew, Hungarian, Italian, Norwegian, Polish, Portuguese Brasilian, Romanian, Russian, Serbian, Slovak, Slovenian, Spanish, Swedish, Ukrainian, Vietnamese.\n         <br/>\n         If you are interested in providing a language support please do a pull request with a json file into the i18n directory.\n         <br/>\n         this is what a language json looks like.\n         <pre class="ssh-pre my-2" data-type="json"><span class="punctuation">{</span>\n  <span class="quote">"weekDays"</span><span class="quote">"Create an event"</span><span class="punctuation">,</span>\n  <span class="quote">"dateFormat"</span><span class="punctuation">:</span> <span class="quote">"DDDD d mmmm yyyy"</span>\n<span class="punctuation">}</span></pre>\n         <p>\n          Regarding the\n          <span class="code">\n           dateFormat\n          </span>\n          translation, this is the format of the full\ndate you can see in a single day view title.\n          <br/>\n          <span class="code">\n           DDDD\n          </span>\n          stands for the full-letter day of week,\n          <span class="code">\n           mmmm\n          </span>\n          stands for\nfull-letter month,\n          <span class="code">\n           d\n          </span>\n          stands for the date of the month (0-31),\n          <span class="code">\n           yyyy\n          </span>\n          stands for full year,\n          <span class="code">\n           {S}\n          </span>\n          stands for st/nd/rd/th and only in English.\n         </p>\n        </p>\n        <p class="highlight tips">\n         <i aria-hidden="true" class="v-icon material-icons theme--light">\n          wb_incandescent\n         </i>\n         Note that 2 media queries will shorten the days of the week to 3 letters then 1 letter when it does not fit.\n         <br/>\n         You can read more about it in the # Responsiveness &amp; Media Queries section in the\n         <a href="#css-notes">\n          CSS Notes\n         </a>\n         .\n        </p>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <code class="mr-2">\n         hideViewSelector\n        </code>\n        <span class="code">\n         [Boolean], default: false\n        </span>\n        <p>\n         When set to true, the top view selector will disappear.\n         <br/>\n         You can still navigate from a view to another by clicking a cell (narrower view) or\nthe view title (broader view).\n        </p>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <code class="mr-2">\n         hideTitleBar\n        </code>\n        <span class="code">\n         [Boolean], default: false\n        </span>\n        <p>\n         When set to true, the title bar with navigating arrows will disappear.\n         <br/>\n         You can still navigate from a view to another with the view selector and clicking\na cell (narrower view).\n        </p>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <code class="mr-2">\n         hideBody\n        </code>\n        <span class="code">\n         [Boolean], default: false\n        </span>\n        <p>\n         When set to true, the whole calendar body will disappear - cells and timeline.\n         <br/>\n         Also means that all the logic usually triggered from the calendar\'s body won\'t run at all.\n        </p>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <code class="mr-2">\n         hideWeekends\n        </code>\n        <span class="code">\n         [Boolean], default: false\n        </span>\n        <p>\n         Hide the weekend and shows only Monday to Friday on month view and week view.\n         <br/>\n         The weekend are still visible in day view not to break the behavior of the arrows.\n         <br/>\n         Note that by hiding the arrows you won\'t be able to see a weekend day in day view if hideWeekends is true.\n        </p>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <code class="mr-2">\n         disableViews\n        </code>\n        <span class="code">\n         [Array], default: []\n        </span>\n        <p>\n         Allows you to totally disable one or more of the available views.\n         <br/>\n         Accepted view names are \'years\', \'year\', \'month\', \'week\', \'day\'.\n         <br/>\n         Note that the navigation between views via cells click or title click won\'t\nbreak and will only navigate to views you have allowed.\n        </p>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <code class="mr-2">\n         defaultView\n        </code>\n        <span class="code">\n         [String], default: \'week\'\n        </span>\n        <p>\n         Allows you to set a default view, for the first time you load the calendar.\n         <br/>\n         Accepts one of \'years\', \'year\', \'month\', \'week\', \'day\'.\n        </p>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <code class="mr-2">\n         todayButton\n        </code>\n        <span class="code">\n         [Boolean], default: false\n        </span>\n        <p>\n         Adds a Today button in the title bar to quickly go to Today\'s date.\n         <br/>\n        </p>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <code class="mr-2">\n         selectedDate\n        </code>\n        <span class="code">\n         [String, Date], default: \'\'\n        </span>\n        <p>\n         Accepts a formatted string or plain JS Date object.\n         <br/>\n         Set a selected date, for the first time you load the calendar.\n         <br/>\n         This day will be highlighted and the first view will naturally show this date.\n         <br/>\n         E.g. setting a date in year 2000 with a defaultView of week, will show you that week of year 2000.\n         <br/>\n         <br/>\n         Updating the\n         <span class="code">\n          selectedDate\n         </span>\n         programmatically after the first calendar load,\nwill update the view if needed to show this date.\n         <br/>\n         Refer to the\n         <a href="#ex--sync-two-calendars">\n          Sync two vue-cal instances\n         </a>\n         example.\n        </p>\n        <p class="highlight warning">\n         <i aria-hidden="true" class="v-icon material-icons theme--light">\n          priority_high\n         </i>\n         A correct string date format is\n         <code>\n          2019-06-09 11:56\n         </code>\n         or\n         <code>\n          2019-06-09\n         </code>\n         if you don\'t need the time.\nOnly these formats will work in string. You can also provide a native Javascript Date object.\n        </p>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <code class="mr-2">\n         minD\x08ate\n        </code>\n        <span class="code">\n         [String, Date], default: \'\'\n        </span>\n        <p>\n         Accepts a formatted string or plain JS Date object.\n         <br/>\n         Set a minimum date for the cells to be selectable.\n         <br/>\n         By default the cell will be grayed out when out of range but CSS classes let you customize this.\n        </p>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <code class="mr-2">\n         maxD\x08ate\n        </code>\n        <span class="code">\n         [String, Date], default: \'\'\n        </span>\n        <p>\n         Accepts a formatted string or plain JS Date object.\n         <br/>\n         Set a maximum date for the cells to be selectable.\n         <br/>\n         By default the cell will be grayed out when out of range but CSS classes let you customize this.\n        </p>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <code class="mr-2">\n         startWeekOnSunday\n        </code>\n        <span class="code">\n         [Boolean], default: false\n        </span>\n        <p>\n         By default weeks start on Monday but with this option you can start the week on Sunday.\n        </p>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <code class="mr-2">\n         small\n        </code>\n        <span class="code">\n         [Boolean], default: false\n        </span>\n        <p>\n         When set to\n         <span class="code">\n          true\n         </span>\n         , the days of the week headings will be truncated to 3 letters.\n         <br/>\n         Does not apply to the title of the day view.\n         <br/>\n         2 media queries are truncating the days of the week bellow 450px,\nread on in the\n         <a href="#css-notes">\n          CSS Notes\n         </a>\n         .\n        </p>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <code class="mr-2">\n         xsmall\n        </code>\n        <span class="code">\n         [Boolean], default: false\n        </span>\n        <p>\n         When set to true, the days of the week headings will be truncated to 1 letter.\n         <br/>\n         Does not apply to the title of the day view.\n         <br/>\n         In Addition, the whole calendar gets applied a smaller font size of 0.9em,\nand the current view title is also reduced.\n         <br/>\n         2 media queries are truncating the days of the week bellow 450px,\nread on in the\n         <a href="#css-notes">\n          CSS Notes\n         </a>\n         .\n        </p>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <code class="mr-2">\n         transitions\n        </code>\n        <span class="code">\n         [Boolean], default: true\n        </span>\n        <p>\n         Enable / disable the CSS transitions between all the views and view states.\n        </p>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <code class="mr-2">\n         clickToNavigate\n        </code>\n        <span class="code">\n         [Boolean], default: false\n        </span>\n        <p>\n         When set to true a single click (or tap for touch devices) will take you to a narrower view if available.\n         <br/>\n         You can always go back to a broader view by clicking the view title or selecting another view from the view selector if enabled.\n         <br/>\n         The navigation to narrower view can be disabled by setting both\n         <span class="code">\n          clickToNavigate\n         </span>\n         and\n         <span class="code">\n          dblClickToNavigate\n         </span>\n         to false.\n        </p>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <code class="mr-2">\n         dblClickToNavigate\n        </code>\n        <span class="code">\n         [Boolean], default: true\n        </span>\n        <p>\n         When set to true a double click (or double tap for touch devices) will take you to a narrower view if available.\n         <br/>\n         You can always go back to a broader view by clicking the view title or selecting another view from the view selector if enabled.\n         <br/>\n         The navigation to narrower view can be disabled by setting both\n         <span class="code">\n          clickToNavigate\n         </span>\n         and\n         <span class="code">\n          dblClickToNavigate\n         </span>\n         to false.\n        </p>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <code class="mr-2">\n         time\n        </code>\n        <span class="code">\n         [Boolean], default: true\n        </span>\n        <p>\n         Whether you want to display the timeline and handle events with time or only date.\n         <br/>\n         Note that time is made of\n         <span class="code">\n          hours:minutes\n         </span>\n         <strong class="ml-2">\n          and no second\n         </strong>\n         .\n        </p>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <code class="mr-2">\n         timeFrom\n        </code>\n        <span class="code">\n         [Number], default: 0\n        </span>\n        <p>\n         If\n         <span class="code">\n          time\n         </span>\n         is enabled, set the start of the timeline in minutes.\nBy default it starts at midnight.\n        </p>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <code class="mr-2">\n         timeTo\n        </code>\n        <span class="code">\n         [Number], default: 24 * 60\n        </span>\n        <p>\n         If\n         <span class="code">\n          time\n         </span>\n         is enabled, set the end of the timeline in minutes.\nBy default it ends at 23.59.\n        </p>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <code class="mr-2">\n         timeStep\n        </code>\n        <span class="code">\n         [Number], default: 30\n        </span>\n        <p>\n         If\n         <span class="code">\n          time\n         </span>\n         is enabled, set the time increment in minutes.\n        </p>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <code class="mr-2">\n         timeCellHeight\n        </code>\n        <span class="code">\n         [Number], default: 40\n        </span>\n        <p>\n         If\n         <span class="code">\n          time\n         </span>\n         is enabled, set the time cell height in pixels.\n         <br/>\n         this is very important as it is used to calculate the events position in the day.\n        </p>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <code class="mr-2">\n         12Hour\n        </code>\n        <span class="code">\n         [Boolean], default: false\n        </span>\n        <p>\n         If\n         <span class="code">\n          time\n         </span>\n         is enabled, the default time format is 24hour.\n         <br/>\n         With\n         <span class="code">\n          12Hour\n         </span>\n         set to true (use\n         <span class="code">\n          12-hour\n         </span>\n         in template),\nthe time format will show 12 hours suffixed with am/pm.\n        </p>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <code class="mr-2">\n         timeFormat\n        </code>\n        <span class="code">\n         [String], default: \'\'\n        </span>\n        <p class="mb-2">\n         When defined, overrides the default time format in time cells and events.\n         <br/>\n         Formatted time can contain any character but the following characters will be replaced:\n        </p>\n        <ul class="ml-3">\n         <li>\n          <strong class="code">\n           H\n          </strong>\n          : Hours no leading zero, 24-hour format\n         </li>\n         <li>\n          <strong class="code">\n           HH\n          </strong>\n          : Hours with leading zero, 24-hour format\n         </li>\n         <li>\n          <strong class="code">\n           h\n          </strong>\n          : Hours no leading zero, 12-hour format\n         </li>\n         <li>\n          <strong class="code">\n           hh\n          </strong>\n          : Hours with leading zero, 12-hour format\n         </li>\n         <li>\n          <strong class="code">\n           m\n          </strong>\n          : Minutes no leading zero\n         </li>\n         <li>\n          <strong class="code">\n           mm\n          </strong>\n          : Minutes with leading zero\n         </li>\n         <li>\n          <strong class="code">\n           {am}\n          </strong>\n          : am or pm\n         </li>\n         <li>\n          The characters\n          <strong class="code">\n           {\n          </strong>\n          ,\n          <strong class="code">\n           }\n          </strong>\n          are removed and used only to\nseparate characters with no space.\n          <br/>\n          E.g.\n          <span class="code">\n           "h:mm{am}"\n          </span>\n          .\n         </li>\n        </ul>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <code class="mr-2">\n         minCellWidth\n        </code>\n        <span class="code">\n         [Number], default: 0\n        </span>\n        <p>\n         In the current version, this is for day splits only.\n         <br/>\n         When a number is set, in pixels, the calendar body will have a horizontal\nscrollbar if the cells don\'t fit naturally in the calendar container.\n        </p>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <code class="mr-2">\n         splitDays\n        </code>\n        <span class="code">\n         [Array], default: []\n        </span>\n        <p>\n         Split each day into multiple vertical splits.\n         <br/>\n         Accepts an array of split objects with attributes.\n         <br/>\n         Each split object can have these attributes:\n         <span class="code">\n          { class: \'string\', label: \'string\' }\n         </span>\n        </p>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <code class="mr-2">\n         editableEvents\n        </code>\n        <span class="code">\n         [Boolean], default: false\n        </span>\n        <p>\n         When\n         <span class="code">\n          editableEvents\n         </span>\n         set to true, allows:\n         <ul>\n          <li>\n           Dragging events (this feature is coming soon)\n          </li>\n          <li>\n           Resizing events by dragging the handle showing at the bottom of each event if\n           <span class="code">\n            time\n           </span>\n           is set to true,\n          </li>\n          <li>\n           Deleting events by click and hold an event\n          </li>\n          <li>\n           Editing events title\n          </li>\n         </ul>\n        </p>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <code class="mr-2">\n         noEventOverlaps\n        </code>\n        <span class="code">\n         [Boolean], default: false\n        </span>\n        <p>\n         When\n         <span class="code">\n          noEventOverlaps\n         </span>\n         is set to true, all the overlapping events will not\noverlap but instead split the cell width in 2 or 3.\n        </p>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <code class="mr-2">\n         eventsOnMonthView\n        </code>\n        <span class="code">\n         [Boolean, String], default: false\n        </span>\n        <p>\n         When set to true, the events will also be displayed on month view\n(including events from visible out of scope days).\n         <br/>\n         When set to the string \'\n         <span class="code">\n          short\n         </span>\n         \', only the event\'s title will be displayed.\n        </p>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <code class="mr-2">\n         eventsCountOnYearView\n        </code>\n        <span class="code">\n         [Boolean], default: false\n        </span>\n        <p>\n         When set to true, the events count will also be displayed on\n         <span class="code">\n          years\n         </span>\n         &amp;\n         <span class="code">\n          year\n         </span>\n         views.\n        </p>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <code class="mr-2">\n         showAllDayEvents\n        </code>\n        <span class="code">\n         [Boolean, String], default: false\n        </span>\n        <ul>\n         <li class="mb-2">\n          When the\n          <span class="code">\n           showAllDayEvents\n          </span>\n          is set to\n          <span class="code">\n           true\n          </span>\n          the events with an\n          <span class="code">\n           allDay\n          </span>\n          attribute set to\n          <span class="code">\n           true\n          </span>\n          will be displayed in a fixed top\nbar on the\n          <span class="code">\n           week\n          </span>\n          &amp;\n          <span class="code">\n           day\n          </span>\n          views.\n          <br/>\n          The all day events bar will only show up if the options\n          <span class="code">\n           showAllDayEvents\n          </span>\n          &amp;\n          <span class="code">\n           time\n          </span>\n          are set to\n          <span class="code">\n           true\n          </span>\n          .\n          <br/>\n          <span class="code">\n           time\n          </span>\n          is important since without time information every event is an all-day\nevent there is no point in separating them then.\n         </li>\n         <li class="mb-2">\n          When\n          <span class="code">\n           showAllDayEvents\n          </span>\n          is set to\n          <span class="code">\n           false\n          </span>\n          , all the all day events\n(\n          <span class="code">\n           allDay\n          </span>\n          attribute set to\n          <span class="code">\n           true\n          </span>\n          ), will show up as a normal\nbackground event.\n         </li>\n         <li class="mb-2">\n          On month view, switching\n          <span class="code">\n           showAllDayEvents\n          </span>\n          on and off will not have any impact\nsince both should display the all day events.\n         </li>\n         <li class="mb-2">\n          <span class="code">\n           showAllDayEvents\n          </span>\n          accepts a\n          <span class="code">\n           Boolean\n          </span>\n          or the string\n          <span class="code">\n           \'short\'\n          </span>\n          , to display only the event title.\n         </li>\n        </ul>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <code class="mr-2">\n         onEventClick\n        </code>\n        <span class="code">\n         [Function], default: null\n        </span>\n        <p>\n         A callback function to execute when an event is clicked.\n         <br/>\n         this function receives 2 parameters:\n         <span class="code">\n          event\n         </span>\n         , the clicked calendar event,\nand\n         <span class="code">\n          e\n         </span>\n         , the associated JavaScript DOM event.\n        </p>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <code class="mr-2">\n         onEventDblclick\n        </code>\n        <span class="code">\n         [Function], default: null\n        </span>\n        <p>\n         A callback function to execute when an event is double clicked.\n         <br/>\n         this function receives 2 parameters:\n         <span class="code">\n          event\n         </span>\n         , the double clicked calendar event,\nand\n         <span class="code">\n          e\n         </span>\n         , the associated JavaScript DOM event.\n        </p>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <code class="mr-2">\n         onEventCreate\n        </code>\n        <span class="code">\n         [Function], default: null\n        </span>\n        <p>\n         A callback function to execute when an event is created.\n         <br/>\n         this function receives 2 parameters:\n         <span class="code">\n          event\n         </span>\n         , the created event,\nand\n         <span class="code">\n          deleteEvent\n         </span>\n         , a function to delete the created event.\n        </p>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <code class="mr-2">\n         events\n        </code>\n        <span class="code">\n         [Array], default: []\n        </span>\n        <p>\n         Allows you to place events in the calendar.\n         <br/>\n         Accepts an array of event objects.\n         <br/>\n         This is what an event object must look like:\n        </p>\n        <p>\n         <pre class="ssh-pre mt-2" data-type="js"><span class="punctuation">{</span>\n  <span class="variable">start</span><span class="punctuation">:</span> <span class="quote">\'2018-11-19 12:00\'</span><span class="punctuation">,</span> <span class="comment">// Required.</span>\n  <span class="variable">end</span><span class="punctuation">:</span> <span class="quote">\'2018-11-19 14:00\'</span><span class="punctuation">,</span> <span class="comment">// Required.</span>\n  <span class="variable">title</span><span class="punctuation">:</span> <span class="quote">\'String\'</span><span class="punctuation">,</span> <span class="comment">// Optional.</span>\n  <span class="variable">content</span><span class="punctuation">:</span> <span class="quote">\'String\'</span><span class="punctuation">,</span> <span class="comment">// Optional.</span>\n  <span class="variable">class</span><span class="punctuation">:</span> <span class="quote">\'String\'</span><span class="punctuation">,</span> <span class="comment">// Optional.</span>\n  <span class="variable">background</span><span class="punctuation">:</span> <span class="punctuation">[</span><span class="keyword">Boolean</span><span class="punctuation">]</span> <span class="comment">// Optional. (Event type not CSS property)</span>\n  <span class="variable">split</span><span class="punctuation">:</span> <span class="punctuation">[</span><span class="keyword">Number</span><span class="punctuation">]</span> <span class="comment">// Optional.</span>\n  <span class="variable">allDay</span><span class="punctuation">:</span> <span class="punctuation">[</span><span class="keyword">Boolean</span><span class="punctuation">]</span> <span class="comment">// Optional.</span>\n<span class="punctuation">}</span></pre>\n         <ul>\n          <li>\n           If no\n           <span class="code">\n            title\n           </span>\n           is provided, no title will be displayed.\n          </li>\n          <li>\n           <span class="code">\n            content\n           </span>\n           accepts free HTML, for instance:\n\'&lt;i class="v-icon material-icons"&gt;local_hospital&lt;/i&gt;\'.\n           <br/>\n           If no\n           <span class="code">\n            content\n           </span>\n           is provided, no content will be displayed.\n          </li>\n          <li>\n           You may need an event CSS\n           <span class="code">\n            class\n           </span>\n           to handle different event types\nfor instance. With different classes you can apply different styles to the events.\n           <br/>\n           E.g. backgrounds, images, borders, etc.\n          </li>\n          <li>\n           The\n           <span class="code">\n            background\n           </span>\n           attribute sets an event as a background event,\nwhich allows overlapping and disable the ability to drag &amp; resize.\n          </li>\n          <li>\n           When using\n           <span class="code">\n            splitDays\n           </span>\n           , the\n           <span class="code">\n            split\n           </span>\n           attribute accepts a number,\nstarting from 1, corresponding to the split you want the event to appear in.\n          </li>\n          <li>\n           When the\n           <span class="code">\n            showAllDayEvents\n           </span>\n           and\n           <span class="code">\n            time\n           </span>\n           options are set to true,\nall the events with an attribute\n           <span class="code">\n            allDay\n           </span>\n           set to true will show up in a\nfixed bar (week &amp; day views).\n          </li>\n         </ul>\n        </p>\n        <p class="highlight warning">\n         <i aria-hidden="true" class="v-icon material-icons theme--light">\n          priority_high\n         </i>\n         <ul>\n          <li>\n           <strong>\n            The events are internally identified by the key\n            <span class="code">\n             `_eid`\n            </span>\n            . This is a reserved keyword.\n           </strong>\n          </li>\n          <li class="mt-2">\n           Correct date formats are\n           <code>\n            2019-06-09 11:56\n           </code>\n           or\n           <code>\n            2019-06-09\n           </code>\n           if you don\'t want any time in the whole calendar.\nOnly these formats will work.\n           <br/>\n           <strong>\n            You can\'t mix events with time and events without, and you can only remove time if the time option is set to false.\n           </strong>\n          </li>\n         </ul>\n        </p>\n       </li>\n      </ul>\n      <h2 class="headline mt-5 pt-5">\n       <a href="#css-notes">\n        CSS Notes\n       </a>\n       <a id="css-notes" name="css-notes">\n       </a>\n      </h2>\n      <p>\n       You can easily change the calendar design with CSS.\n      </p>\n      <h3 class="mt-5">\n       # Color &amp; rounded Themes\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       Currently 2 color themes (green &amp; blue) are available, in addition to the standard grey theme.\n       <br/>\n       You can apply a green or blue theme by using the CSS class\n       <span class="code">\n        vuecal--green-theme\n       </span>\n       or\n       <span class="code">\n        vuecal--blue-theme\n       </span>\n       .\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       If you want another color theme, you can define your own easily.\n       <br/>\n       This is what a standard color theme looks like.\nYou can copy and change any color to quickly get a nice render.\n       <br/>\n       If that is still not doing what you want you can change even more in your own CSS.\n      </p>\n      <pre class="ssh-pre" data-label="CSS" data-type="css"><span class="comment">/* Green-theme. */</span><span class="selector">\n.vuecal__menu, .vuecal__cell-events-count </span><span class="punctuation">{</span><span class="attribute keyword">background-color</span><span class="punctuation">:</span> <span class="color" style="background-color: #42b983;color: #000">#42b983</span><span class="punctuation">;}</span><span class="selector">\n.vuecal__menu li </span><span class="punctuation">;</span><span class="attribute keyword">color</span><span class="punctuation">:</span> <span class="color" style="background-color: #fff;color: #000">#fff</span><span class="punctuation">;}</span><span class="selector">\n.vuecal__menu li.active </span><span class="punctuation">{</span><span class="attribute keyword">background-color</span><span class="punctuation">:</span> <span class="color" style="background-color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.15);color: #000">rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.15)</span><span class="punctuation">;}</span><span class="selector">\n.vuecal__title-bar </span><span class="punctuation">{</span><span class="attribute keyword">background-color</span><span class="punctuation">:</span> <span class="color" style="background-color: #e4f5ef;color: #000">#e4f5ef</span><span class="punctuation">;}</span><span class="selector">\n.vuecal__cell.today, .vuecal__cell.current </span><span class="punctuation">{</span><span class="attribute keyword">background-color</span><span class="punctuation">:</span> <span class="color" style="background-color: rgba(240, 240, 255, 0.4);color: #000">rgba(240, 240, 255, 0.4)</span><span class="punctuation">;}</span>\n.<span class="attribute">vuecal</span><span class="punctuation">:</span>not<span class="punctuation">(</span>.vuecal--day-view<span class="punctuation">)</span><span class="selector"> .vuecal__cell.selected </span><span class="punctuation">{</span><span class="attribute keyword">background-color</span><span class="punctuation">:</span> <span class="color" style="background-color: rgba(235, 255, 245, 0.4);color: #000">rgba(235, 255, 245, 0.4)</span><span class="punctuation">;}</span><span class="selector">\n.vuecal__cell.selected:before </span><span class="punctuation">{</span><span class="attribute keyword">border-color</span><span    <strong>\n        Rounded Theme\n        <br/>\n       </strong>\n       You can use the rounded cells theme like in the Example\n       <a href="#ex--calendar-themes">\n        Calendar themes - Rounded cells\n       </a>\n       ,\nby applying the CSS class\n       <span class="code">\n        vuecal--rounded-theme\n       </span>\n       to the Vue Cal wrapper.\n      </p>\n      <h3 class="mt-5">\n       # Responsiveness &amp; Media Queries\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       This calendar is fully responsive.\n       <br/>\n       To help you in making the calendar always look perfect,\n2 media queries (to keep it simple) are in place for small screens.\n       <br/>\n       The media queries operate downward from 550px &amp; 450px, to truncate the text\nof the days of the week from full day name to 3 letters and to 1 letter according to the available space.\n       <br/>\n       <br/>\n       If this is not enough for your particular use, you can add your own in your CSS.\n       <br/>\n       Additionally, you can use the options\n       <span class="code">\n        small\n       </span>\n       &amp;\n       <span class="code">\n        xsmall\n       </span>\n       to truncate week days at any size.\n      </p>\n      <h3 class="mt-5">\n       # Disabled Text Selection\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       By default the selection is disabled in the whole calendar except in the events.\nyou can override this by CSS.\n      </p>\n      <h2 class="headline mt-5 pt-5 mb-2">\n       <a href="#release-notes">\n        Release Notes\n       </a>\n       <a
